plane-crazy 2022-09-16 16:04:25 https://streamable.com/0i16gr

Blue motors set the angle of the segment. Speed of each blue motor increases by 0.1 for each extra segment. (1st segment is 0.1, 2nd is 0.2, 3rd is 0.3, etc.) Pink motor spins the whole thing after locking it in place. Every motor that isn't pink or blue is for locking in place. The bigger the wheel, the more segments you need.
